DisableServerHTTPTimeouts(next http.Handler) http.Handler {\n424: \treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n425: \t\tc := http.NewResponseController(w)\n426: \t\tzero := time.Time{}\n427: \n428: \t\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"disabling HTTP server timeouts for URL\", \"url\", r.URL)\n429: \n430: \t\tif err := c.SetReadDeadline(zero); err != nil {\n431: \t\t\tlevel.Warn(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"failed to clear write deadline on HTTP connection\", \"url\", r.URL, \"err\", err)\n435: \t\t}\n436: \n437: \t\tnext.ServeHTTP(w, r)\n438: \t})\n439: }\n440:
